SELECT p."Id", p."Nombre", p.stock, t."CategoriasId", t."ProductosId", t."Id", t."NivelId", t."Nombre"
FROM "Producto" AS p
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c."CategoriasId", c."ProductosId", c0."Id", c0."NivelId", c0."Nombre"
    FROM "CategoriaProducto" AS c
    INNER JOIN "Categoria" AS c0 ON c."CategoriasId" = c0."Id"
) AS t ON p."Id" = t."ProductosId"
ORDER BY p."Id", t."CategoriasId", t."ProductosId", t."Id"

SELECT p."Id", p."Nombre", p.stock, t."CategoriasId", t."ProductosId", t."Id", t."NivelId", t."Nombre", t."Id0", t."Nombre0"
FROM "Producto" AS p
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c."CategoriasId", c."ProductosId", c0."Id", c0."NivelId", c0."Nombre", n."Id" AS "Id0", n."Nombre" AS "Nombre0"
    FROM "CategoriaProducto" AS c
    INNER JOIN "Categoria" AS c0 ON c."CategoriasId" = c0."Id"
    LEFT JOIN "Nivel" AS n ON c0."NivelId" = n."Id"
) AS t ON p."Id" = t."ProductosId"
ORDER BY p."Id", t."CategoriasId", t."ProductosId", t."Id", t."Id0"

SELECT p."Id", p."Nombre", p.stock, t."CategoriasId", t."ProductosId", t."Id", t."NivelId", t."Nombre", t."Id0", t."Nombre0"
FROM "Producto" AS p
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c."CategoriasId", c."ProductosId", c0."Id", c0."NivelId", c0."Nombre", n."Id" AS "Id0", n."Nombre" AS "Nombre0"
    FROM "CategoriaProducto" AS c
    INNER JOIN "Categoria" AS c0 ON c."CategoriasId" = c0."Id"
    LEFT JOIN "Nivel" AS n ON c0."NivelId" = n."Id"
) AS t ON p."Id" = t."ProductosId"
WHERE p.stock >= 10
ORDER BY p.stock DESC, p."Id", t."CategoriasId", t."ProductosId", t."Id", t."Id0"

WHERE NOT (a."IsAbandoned") AND (a."NextTryTime" <= @__Now_0)
ORDER BY a."Priority" DESC, a."TryCount", a."NextTryTime"
LIMIT @__p_1
